 chapter 1 chained to a cavern wall , adrien hung forward from his shackles , arms shaking .

 `` what feeds us in the midst of destruction ? ''

 `` blood ! ''

 * * * as darkness fell , and with a lantern in hand , lily haven moved up the path that led to the secret cavern prison .
